msg:As an award-winning B&B, it is indeed well designed. After staying there for four days, the summary is as follows:
Advantages: The villa area is very quiet and you can see Erhai Lake from the third and fourth floors. Each room is over 80 square meters and is large enough. There is afternoon tea and evening milk every day. Drinks in the refrigerator are also free. There is also a free pick-up and drop-off service, and bed sheets and quilt covers will be changed every two days.
Disadvantages: Afternoon tea is repeated every day, and you will inevitably get tired of it if you eat too much. Breakfast is also the same every day with no choice of set menu. There are many electrical appliances in the house, but there are no specific operating instructions, so you need to explore by yourself. The lobby is on the second floor and requires climbing stairs every day, which is not friendly to some people. The fresh air system has a button but it doesn't work. The price is higher than that of a five-star suite, but the price/performance ratio is slightly lower.
